estate_artificers_organization_international_gommo = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				has_country_flag = nsc_sun_elf_artificery
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					was_tag = Y20
					tag = Y20
				}
				mission_completed = feiten_shuimu_engineering_cadre
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_artificers_special_organization_privilege = yes }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = artificers_regular_organization_locked }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = artificers_currently_choosing_organization } #To not allow player start reaserch and change organization - only on base privileges
	}
	can_select = {
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes }
			
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				dip_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				dip_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = five_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = artifice_research_fast
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = five_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_artificers_organization_international_gommo }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_dip_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_dip_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_artificers_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = artifice_research_fast
		}
		#hidden_effect = {
		#	add_country_modifier = {
		#		name = rajput_to_artificer
		#		duration = -1
		#		hidden = yes
		#	}
		#}
	}
	mechanics = {
        enables_rajput_regiments
    }
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

estate_artificers_organization_state = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.1
	land_share = 0
	is_valid = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				has_country_flag = nsc_sun_elf_artificery
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_estate = estate_dragon_command }
			has_institution = manufactories
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					was_tag = Y20
					tag = Y20
				}
				mission_completed = feiten_shuimu_engineering_cadre
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_artificers_special_organization_privilege = yes }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = artificers_regular_organization_locked }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = artificers_currently_choosing_organization } #To not allow player start reaserch and change organization - only on base privileges
	}
	can_select = {
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes }
			
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 30
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				dip_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				dip_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = fifteen_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = artifice_research_slow
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = fifteen_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_artificers_organization_state }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_dip_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_dip_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_artificers_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = artifice_research_slow
		}
		#hidden_effect = {
		#	add_country_modifier = {
		#		name = rajput_to_artificer
		#		duration = -1
		#		hidden = yes
		#	}
		#}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_year = 1445 }
				}
				take_estate_land_share_massive = { estate = estate_artificers }
			}
		}
	}
	mechanics = {
        enables_rajput_regiments
    }
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			current_age = age_of_absolutism
		}
	}
}

estate_artificers_organization_ravelian_control = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = 0
	#Removed this so AI doesn't sit at negative mages loyalty
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		religion = ravelian
		NOT = { has_artificers_special_organization_privilege = yes }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = artificers_currently_choosing_organization } #To not allow player start reaserch and change organization - only on base privileges
	}
	can_select = {
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				dip_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				dip_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = ten_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = artifice_research_normal
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = ten_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_artificers_organization_ravelian_control }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_dip_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_dip_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_artificers_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = artifice_research_normal
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_ravelian_control_invalid_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes } }
				set_estate_privilege = estate_artificers_organization_state
			}
		}
	}
	mechanics = {
        enables_rajput_regiments
    }
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		global_missionary_strength = 0.02
		church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
		church_influence_modifier = 0.05
		
		papal_influence = 0.5
		allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

estate_artificers_organization_sun_elf = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	influence = -0.10
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	is_valid = {
		is_chosen_country = yes
		OR = {
			religion = bulwari_sun_cult
			has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window
		}
		NOT = { has_artificers_special_organization_privilege = yes }
	}
	on_invalid = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_sun_elf_artificery
		country_event = { id = estate_organization.5 }
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_artificers
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				dip_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				dip_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = ten_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		clr_country_flag = nsc_sun_elf_artificery
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = artifice_research_normal
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = ten_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_artificers_organization_sun_elf }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_dip_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_dip_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_artificers_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = artifice_research_normal
		}
	}
	mechanics = {
        enables_rajput_regiments
    }
	penalties = {
		global_unrest = 1
		artificers_capacity = -5
	}
	benefits = {
		nobles_influence_modifier = 0.10
		allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

estate_artificers_organization_feiten_shuimu_cadre = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.15
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			tag = Y20
			was_tag = Y20
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		OR = {
			tag = Y20
			was_tag = Y20
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = ten_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		custom_tooltip = estate_artificers_organization_feiten_shuimu_cadre_provides_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = feiten_province_balance
							value = 0.001
						}
					}
				}
			}
			tooltip = { add_country_modifier = { name = feiten_shuimu_regiments_below_cap duration = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 0.001
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = feiten_province_balance
							value = 0.5001
						}
					}
				}
			}
			tooltip = { add_country_modifier = { name = feiten_shuimu_regiments_slightly_above_cap duration = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 0.5001
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = feiten_province_balance
							value = 1.001
						}
					}
				}
			}
			tooltip = { add_country_modifier = { name = feiten_shuimu_regiments_above_cap duration = -1 } }
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = { add_country_modifier = { name = feiten_shuimu_regiments_way_over_cap duration = -1 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = artifice_research_normal
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = ten_year_artifice_research_tt
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		clear_artificers_organization_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_year = 1445 }
				}
				take_estate_land_share_massive = { estate = estate_artificers }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = artifice_research_normal
		}
	}
	mechanics = { enables_rajput_regiments }
	penalties = { }
	benefits = { }
	# Below cap
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 0.001
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			siege_ability = 0.2
			ship_power_propagation = 0.2
			movement_speed_in_fleet_modifier = 2
			allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.025
			naval_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
			fire_damage_received = 0.2 # Balloons/airships blowing/burning up result in lots of collateral damage
		}
	}
	# 0% to 50% over cap
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feiten_province_balance
					value = 0.001
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 0.5001
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			siege_ability = 0.15
			ship_power_propagation = 0.15
			movement_speed_in_fleet_modifier = 1.5
			allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.025
			naval_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
			fire_damage_received = 0.2
		}
	}
	# 50% to 100% over cap
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feiten_province_balance
					value = 0.5001
				}
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 1.001
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			siege_ability = 0.1
			ship_power_propagation = 0.1
			movement_speed_in_fleet_modifier = 1
			allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.025
			naval_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
			fire_damage_received = 0.2
		}
	}
	# >100% over cap
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feiten_province_balance
					value = 1.001
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			siege_ability = 0.05
			ship_power_propagation = 0.05
			movement_speed_in_fleet_modifier = 0.5
			allowed_rajput_fraction = 0.025
			naval_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
			fire_damage_received = 0.2
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

#Gor Vazumbrog Vaultwardens
estate_artificers_organization_vaultwardens = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.2
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		is_or_was_tag = { tag = I14 }
		OR = {
			mission_completed = gor_vazumbrog_history_lessons
			has_institution = manufactories
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gor_vazumbrog_unlock_full_artificery }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = artifice_research_fast
			}
			custom_tooltip = five_year_artifice_research_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = no_artifice_research_tt
			add_country_modifier = { name = artifice_research_temporarily_disabled duration = -1 hidden = yes }
			add_country_modifier = { name = artifice_inventions_temporarily_disabled duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_artificers_organization_vaultwardens }
			}
			clear_artificers_organization_effect = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = may_grant_battlemage_academies
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gor_vazumbrog_golemancy #quality instead of quantity artifice regiments
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gor_vazumbrog_unlock_full_artificery }
			custom_tooltip = five_year_artifice_research_tt
		}
		else = {
		     custom_tooltip = no_artifice_research_tt
		}
		custom_tooltip = artificer_points_hover_over_me_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_research_temporarily_disabled
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_inventions_temporarily_disabled
			clr_country_flag = may_grant_battlemage_academies
			clr_country_flag = artifice_research_fast
		}
		remove_country_modifier = gor_vazumbrog_golemancy
	}
	mechanics = { enables_rajput_regiments }
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

#New Artificer Stuff(Sort?)
estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_damestear
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		damestear = 1
		NOT = { has_country_flag = artifice_no_base_privileges }
	}
	can_select = {
		
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = JY_LF_not_trading #Anbennar
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = JY_LF_recent_trade }
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear }
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_mercantilism = 1
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 8
			trigger = {
				trade_goods = damestear
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_DAMESTEAR_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = damestear
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_revoke_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ANB_estate_artificers_loyalty_refund
			}
			clr_country_flag = ANB_estate_artificers_loyalty_refund
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 20
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_artificers_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.12 }
	}
	ai_will_do = { #having the AI use these could lead to an unstoppable downwards spiral if it can't work out how to get rid of them
		factor = 0
	}
}

		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = artifice_requires_artificery_only_mode_tt
			has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = artifice_ivory_tools_enact_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ivory
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_ivory_tools
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = artifice_ivory_tools_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ANB_estate_artificers_loyalty_refund
			}
			clr_country_flag = ANB_estate_artificers_loyalty_refund
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 20
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = ivory
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_ivory_tools
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = artifice_ivory_tools }
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_ivory_tools
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = artifice_ivory_tools }
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_ivory_tools
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

estate_artificers_feiten_invest_engineering_workshop = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	influence = 0
	loyalty = 0.05
	land_share = 5
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop_unlocked
		# NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_able_to_build_shuimu_extension }
	}
	can_select = {
		any_owned_province = {
			superregion = yanshen_superregion
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop }
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop_no_tech_cost}
			OR = {
				has_building = university
				has_production_building_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = feiten_choose_facility_location_tt
		tooltip = {
			mission_reward_artifice_points_1 = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
						check_variable = {
							which = feiten_number_of_shuimu_engineering_cadre_facilities_investments
							value = 5
						}
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop_no_tech_cost
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_feiten.312
			}
		}
		
		# add_dip_power = -33
		# if = {
		# 	limit = { monthly_income = 40 }
		# 	add_treasury = -500
		# }
		# else = { add_years_of_income = -1 }
		# custom_tooltip = feiten_apply_after_expires_tt
		# tooltip = { mission_reward_artifice_points_1 = yes }
		# random_owned_province = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		superregion = yanshen_superregion
		# 		NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop }
		# 		NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop_no_tech_cost}
		# 		OR = {
		# 			has_building = university
		# 			has_production_building_trigger = yes
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# 	set_province_flag = shuimu_workshop_build_location
		# 	if = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
		# 				check_variable = {
		# 					which = feiten_number_of_shuimu_engineering_cadre_facilities_investments
		# 					value = 5
		# 				}
		# 			}
		# 		}
		# 		tooltip = {
		# 			add_province_modifier = {
		# 				name = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop_no_tech_cost
		# 				duration = -1
		# 			}
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# 	else = {
		# 		tooltip = {
		# 			add_province_modifier = {
		# 				name = feiten_shuimu_engineering_workshop
		# 				duration = -1
		# 			}
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
	
	on_invalid = {
		# hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = feiten_able_to_build_shuimu_extension }
	}
	
	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = { }
	
	# cooldown_years = 5
	# on_cooldown_expires = {
	# 	set_country_flag = feiten_able_to_build_shuimu_extension
	# 	random_owned_province = {

	# 						which = feiten_number_of_shuimu_engineering_cadre_facilities_investments

# Promote Starry-Eye scholars
estate_artificers_feiten_starry_eye_promotion = {
	icon = privilege_send_emissary_to_pope
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	land_share = 0
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	is_valid = { mission_completed = feiten_shuimu_engineering_cadre }
	can_select = { }
	can_revoke = { }
	on_granted = {
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religious_school = {
					group = raheni
					school = starry_eye_school
				}
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = increased_religion_opinion
			}
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religious_school = {
					group = raheni
					school = starry_eye_school
				}
			}
			remove_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = increased_religion_opinion
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_invalid = {
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religious_school = {
					group = raheni
					school = starry_eye_school
				}
			}
			remove_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = increased_religion_opinion
			}
		}
	}
	
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.1
	}
	
	benefits = {
		institution_spread_from_true_faith = 0.2
		innovativeness_gain = 0.25
	}
	
	on_cooldown_expires = { }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

# Grant Foreign Membership
estate_artificers_feiten_grant_foreign_membership = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_inouisitor
	influence = -0.05
	loyalty = -0.05
	land_share = 5
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	is_valid = { mission_completed = feiten_arrival_of_gnomes }
	can_select = { }
	can_revoke = { }
	on_granted = {
		add_prestige = -10
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_any_gnomish_pop_trigger = no }
			add_unrest = 10
			add_gnomish_minority_size_effect = yes
		}
	}

	on_revoked = { }
	
	on_invalid = { }
	
	penalties = {
		global_unrest = 2
		stability_cost_modifier = 0.2
	}
	
	benefits = {
		global_institution_spread = 0.25
		technology_cost = -0.05
	}
	
	cooldown_years = 5
	on_cooldown_expires = { }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

estate_artificers_hyti_labs = {
	icon = privilege_artificers_grand_exhibition_hall
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_privilege_estate_artificers_hyti_labs
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = artifice_inventions.1 }
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = artifice_inventions.1 }
		}
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_capacity = 10
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}
estate_artificers_hyti_peace = {
	icon = privilege_artificers_grand_exhibition_hall
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = -0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_privilege_estate_artificers_hyti_peace
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = hyti_peace_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = artifice_inventions.1 }
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		allowed_rajput_fraction = -0.15
	}
	on_revoked = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = hyti_less_rajput
			duration = 1825
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = artifice_inventions.1 }
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}
estate_artificers_hyti_circle = {
	icon = privilege_artificers_grand_exhibition_hall
	loyalty = 0
	influence = -0.15
	is_valid = {
		has_estate_privilege = estate_artificers_hyti_circle
	}
	can_revoke = { always = no }
	benefits = {	#offset most of the mixed malus until you fully unlock artificery 
		mages_mana_capacity = 80
		mages_mana_regen_mult = 0.3
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = artifice_inventions.1 }
			update_mana_regen_vars = yes change_mana = yes
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = artifice_inventions.1 }
			update_mana_regen_vars = yes change_mana = yes
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = artifice_inventions.1 }
			update_mana_regen_vars = yes change_mana = yes
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		artificers_capacity = -15
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

# Beikdugang


estate_artificers_flamekeepers = {
	icon = privilege_grant_new_world_charter
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			mission_completed = Y15_corner_market
			overlord = { mission_completed = Y15_corner_market }
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		OR = {
			mission_completed = Y15_corner_market
			overlord = { mission_completed = Y15_corner_market }
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_flamekeepers }
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = Y15_flamekeeper_granted
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_climate = arctic }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		add_stability = -1
		custom_tooltip = Y15_flamekeeper_revoked
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = Y15_flamekeeper_revoked
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
	}
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.15
	}
	benefits = {
		naval_attrition = -0.2
		trade_range_modifier = 0.25
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }
}

#inventions

artifice_invention_portable_turrets = {
	icon = Artf_MaMi1
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_portable_turrets
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = artifice_portable_turrets
			duration = -1
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_portable_turrets
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_portable_turrets_tt
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

artifice_invention_chi_cultivation = {
	icon = Artf_TeMi2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_chi_cultivation_charm
		religion = devouring_path
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chi_cultivation
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
		religion = devouring_path
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = artifice_chi_cultivation_charm
			duration = -1
		}
		artifice_granted_20 = yes

	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_chi_cultivation_charm
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_chi_cultivation_charm_tt
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_chi_cultivation_charm
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_chi_cultivation_charm_tt
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_technomancy_influence = 0.04
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = artifice_platinum_warsuit
			duration = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = I08 } #haraz orldhum
			artifice_granted_10 = yes
		}
		else = { artifice_granted_20 = yes }

	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_platinum_warsuit
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_platinum_warsuit_tt
		if = {
			limit = { tag = I08 } #haraz orldhum
			artifice_remove_10 = yes
		}
		else = { artifice_remove_20 = yes }
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_platinum_warsuit
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_platinum_warsuit_tt
		if = {
			limit = { tag = I08 } #haraz orldhum
			artifice_remove_10 = yes
		}
		else = { artifice_remove_20 = yes }
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.06
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_wine_ageifier = {
	icon = Artf_MaEc1
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_wine_ageifier
		culture_group = lencori
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_wine_ageifier
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
		culture_group = lencori
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		# every_owned_province = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		trade_goods = wine
		# 	}
		# 	add_province_modifier = {
		# 		name = artifice_wine_ageifier
		# 		duration = -1
		# 		hidden = yes
		# 	}
		# }
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_wine_ageifier_tt
		tooltip = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_wine_ageifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = wine
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_wine_ageifier
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = artifice_wine_ageifier
			}
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_wine_ageifier
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = artifice_wine_ageifier
			}
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_wine_ageifier
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = artifice_wine_ageifier
			}
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_wine_ageifier
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		
	}
	conditional_modifier = { # Lead by Wine
		trigger = {
			production_leader = { trade_goods = wine }
		}
		modifier = {
			global_unrest = -1
		}
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_technomancy_influence = 0.02
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

#missions
artifice_invention_vg_musket_precursor_edition = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq3
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		mission_completed = vanbury_guild_preliminary_precursor_weaponry_research
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_vg_musket_precursor_edition
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_30 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_30 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = vg_invention_1
					has_country_flag = vg_invention_3
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition }
				remove_country_modifier = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition }
			custom_tooltip = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition_tt
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition }
				remove_country_modifier = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition }
			custom_tooltip = artifice_vg_musket_precursor_edition_tt
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		#foo
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = vg_invention_2
				has_country_flag = vg_invention_3
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			infantry_power = 0.1
			global_regiment_cost = -0.05
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			mission_completed = vanbury_guild_mass_production_of_artificer_weapons
		}
		modifier = {
			infantry_power = 0.2
			global_regiment_cost = -0.1
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered }
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
				clr_province_flag = permanent_precursor_relics
				REB = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = num_precursor_relics
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_from_saved_trade_goods = yes
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered }
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_province_flag = temple_being_plundered
				clr_province_flag = permanent_precursor_relics
				REB = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = num_precursor_relics

					}
				}
			}
			change_trade_goods = unknown
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.1
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		dragon_command_privilege_slots = 1
		#foo
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			NOT = {
				capital_scope = { superregion = vimdatrong_superregion }
				capital_scope = { superregion = yanshen_superregion }
				capital_scope = { superregion = rahen_superregion }
				capital_scope = { superregion = gozengun_superregion }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			religion = high_philosophy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = {
				any_owned_province = {
					province_group = temple_province_group
					NOT = { has_province_flag = already_plundered }
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

	}

artifice_invention_feiten_farsight_telescopes = {
	icon = Artf_BrEc2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_feiten_farsight_telescopes
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_feiten_farsight_telescopes
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
		NOT = { feiten_has_propulsion_invention = yes }
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_feiten_farsight_telescopes_upgraded_tt
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
		custom_tooltip = feiten_revoke_privilege_no_loyalty_penalty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 20
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1

	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			trading_bonus = {
				trade_goods = glass
				value = no
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			movement_speed = 0.1
			naval_attrition = -0.1
			land_attrition = -0.1
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			trading_bonus = {
				trade_goods = glass
				value = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			movement_speed = 0.15
			naval_attrition = -0.2
			land_attrition = -0.2
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_feiten_specialized_construction_arms = {
	icon = Artf_MaEc1
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_feiten_specialized_construction_arms
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_feiten_specialized_construction_arms
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		NOT = { feiten_has_gondola_invention = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_feiten_specialized_construction_arms_upgraded_tt
		custom_tooltip = feiten_aerial_cranes_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				trading_bonus = {
					trade_goods = naval_supplies
					value = yes
				}
			}
			
			tooltip = {
				capital_scope = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = {
				capital_scope = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = mountain
					has_terrain = highlands
					has_terrain = hills
					has_terrain = coastline
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
						trading_bonus = {
							trade_goods = naval_supplies
							value = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod
					has_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod				
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = feiten_revoke_privilege_no_loyalty_penalty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 20
			}
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod
					has_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod				
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod
					has_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod_upgraded
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_specialized_construction_arms_mod				
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1

	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			trading_bonus = {
				trade_goods = naval_supplies
				value = no
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			great_project_upgrade_cost = -0.25
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			trading_bonus = {
				trade_goods = naval_supplies
				value = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			great_project_upgrade_cost = -0.5
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_feiten_skywriting
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_feiten_skywriting
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		NOT = { feiten_has_armaments_invention = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_feiten_skywriting_upgraded_tt
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = feiten_revoke_privilege_no_loyalty_penalty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 20
			}
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			trading_bonus = {
				trade_goods = dyes
				value = no
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			global_unrest = -2
			diplomatic_reputation = 1
			prestige = 1
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			trading_bonus = {
				trade_goods = dyes
				value = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {

artifice_invention_feiten_electroplated_armor = {
	icon = Artf_MaMi3
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_feiten_electroplated_armor
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_feiten_electroplated_armor
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		NOT = { feiten_has_gondola_invention = yes }
		artifice_has_points_30 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_feiten_electroplated_armor_upgraded_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				trading_bonus = {
					trade_goods = copper
					value = yes
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		artifice_granted_30 = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod
			remove_country_modifier = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod_upgraded
		}
		custom_tooltip = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod_tt
		custom_tooltip = feiten_revoke_privilege_no_loyalty_penalty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_artificers
				loyalty = 20
			}
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod
			remove_country_modifier = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod_upgraded
		}
		custom_tooltip = feiten_electroplated_armor_mod_tt
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1

	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = { artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes }
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_korashi_tuners_revoke_tt

		mages_estate_experience_mod = 1
	}

		factor = 25
	}

			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_ameion_lift_generator
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
		custom_tooltip = G52_lift_granted
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = kheionai_ruinborn_elf
				OR = {
					has_terrain = city_terrain
					has_terrain = farmlands
					has_terrain = grasslands
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = G52_lift_generator
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = G52_lift_generator }
			remove_province_modifier = G52_lift_generator
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
		custom_tooltip = G52_lift_revoked
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = G52_lift_generator }
			remove_province_modifier = G52_lift_generator
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = G52_lift_generator }
			remove_province_modifier = G52_lift_generator
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = G52_lift_revoked
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		development_cost = -0.1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_order_inscribed_forges = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_order_inscribed_forges
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_order_inscribed_forges
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_order_inscribed_forges_tt
		tooltip = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_weapons_trade_goods = yes
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
			}
			remove_province_modifier = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
			}
			remove_province_modifier = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
			}
			remove_province_modifier = F78_artifice_order_inscribed_forges
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

#Kobildzan Draconic Ascension
artifice_invention_kobildzan_draconic_ascension = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq1
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_kobildzan_draconic_ascension
	}
	can_select = {
        always = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = upgrading_ascension_tt
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = Z38
					is_subject_of = Z38
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		# NOTE: No artificer points utilized here b/c it depends on the stage of the invention; handled during unlock / upgrade
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = Z38_claws_of_power_regiment_mod
			remove_country_modifier = Z38_ogre_sized_kobolds_regiment_mod
			remove_country_modifier = Z38_malliaths_chosen_disciples_regiment_mod
			remove_country_modifier = Z38_dragonfire_sacs_regiment_mod
			remove_country_modifier = Z38_ebonsteel_shieldscales_regiment_mod
			remove_country_modifier = Z38_the_holiest_flesh_regiment_mod
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = Z38_claws_of_power_regiment_mod }
			custom_tooltip = kobildzan_draconic_ascension_1_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = Z38_ogre_sized_kobolds_regiment_mod }
			custom_tooltip = kobildzan_draconic_ascension_2_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = Z38_malliaths_chosen_disciples_regiment_mod }
			custom_tooltip = kobildzan_draconic_ascension_3_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = Z38_dragonfire_sacs_regiment_mod }
			custom_tooltip = kobildzan_draconic_ascension_4_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = Z38_ebonsteel_shieldscales_regiment_mod }
			custom_tooltip = kobildzan_draconic_ascension_5_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = Z38_the_holiest_flesh_regiment_mod }
			custom_tooltip = kobildzan_draconic_ascension_6_tt
		}
		artifice_remove_dynamic = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		
	}
	benefits = {

#Rezankand
artifice_invention_rezankand_phoenix = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq1
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_rezankand_phoenix
	}
	can_select = {
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = rezankand_phoenix_invention_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = rezankand_phoenix_invention_mod
		}
		custom_tooltip = rezankand_phoenix_invention_mod_tt
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = rezankand_phoenix_invention_mod
		}
		custom_tooltip = rezankand_phoenix_invention_mod_tt
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
		amount_of_hussars = 4
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_light_matrix_supply = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_light_matrix_supply
	}
	can_select = {
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
		custom_tooltip = rezankand_light_matrix_explanation_tt
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rezankand_matrix_invention_upgraded }
			tooltip = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		} 
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = rezankand_light_matrix_supply_removal_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		#foo
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {  owner = { has_country_flag = rezankand_matrix_invention_upgraded } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_building = mage_tower }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply_upgraded
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owned_by = ROOT 
						has_building = mage_tower
					} 
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_building = mage_tower }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply
					duration = -1
				}
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owned_by = ROOT 
						has_building = mage_tower
					} 
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = rezankand_light_matrix_supply
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = rezankand_light_matrix_supply_upgraded }
			remove_province_modifier = rezankand_light_matrix_supply_upgraded
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = rezankand_light_matrix_supply }
			remove_province_modifier = rezankand_light_matrix_supply
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_innate_windshaping
	}
	can_select = {
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes

	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		
	}
	benefits = {
		movement_speed_in_fleet_modifier = 2
		ship_trade_power_modifier = 0.2
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_hanging_houses = {

			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}

	on_revoked = {
		harpy_roost_se_adjust_dev_required = { dev_required_adjustment = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}

	}

	on_invalid = {
		harpy_roost_se_adjust_dev_required = { dev_required_adjustment = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.02
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {

		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_seismic_armor = {
	icon = artifice_invention_reaver_axe_rifle
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_seismic_armor
		is_bulwari_influenced_harpy_culture = yes
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = F98
				mission_completed = F98_elemental_artifice
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = artifice_seismic_armor_mod_harpylen_improved
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = artifice_seismic_armor_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}		
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
	}

	on_revoked = {
		remove_country_modifier = artifice_seismic_armor_mod_harpylen_improved
		remove_country_modifier = artifice_seismic_armor_mod
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}

	on_invalid = {
		remove_country_modifier = artifice_seismic_armor_mod_harpylen_improved
		remove_country_modifier = artifice_seismic_armor_mod
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.04
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_scream_beamers = {
	icon = artifice_invention_reaver_axe_rifle
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_scream_beamers
		is_bulwari_influenced_harpy_culture = yes
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_30 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { mission_completed = F98_elemental_artifice }
			custom_tooltip = scream_beamers_harpylen_tt
			tooltip = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_scream_beamers_mod_harpylen
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = scream_beamers_tt
			tooltip = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_scream_beamers_mod
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_30 = yes
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { province_with_mineable_goods = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { mission_completed = F98_elemental_artifice } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_scream_beamers_mod_harpylen
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_scream_beamers_mod
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_scream_beamers_mod
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_scream_beamers_mod_harpylen		
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = scream_beamers_tt
		tooltip = { remove_province_modifier = artifice_scream_beamers_mod }
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes		
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_scream_beamers_mod
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_scream_beamers_mod_harpylen
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
	}

	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_scream_beamers_mod
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_scream_beamers_mod_harpylen
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_brilliance_influence = 0.06
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_hyti_magiwind = {
	icon = artifice_invention_hyti_magiwind
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_hyti_magiwind
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = hyti_turn_wind_on_tt
		tooltip = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = hyti_magic_trains_on
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = hyti_magic_trains_off }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = hyti_magic_trains_on
					duration = -1
				}
				remove_province_modifier = hyti_magic_trains_off
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_terrain = cavern }
				remove_province_modifier = hyti_cave_mod5
			}
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = hyti_magic_trains_on }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = hyti_magic_trains_off
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = hyti_magic_trains_on
		}
		every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_terrain = cavern }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = hyti_cave_mod5
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = hyti_magic_trains_on }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = hyti_magic_trains_off
					duration = -1
				}
				remove_province_modifier = hyti_magic_trains_on
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_terrain = cavern }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = hyti_cave_mod5
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_brilliance_influence = 0.02
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation = {
	icon = Artf_MaEc2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
		is_bulwari_or_zanlibi_culture = yes
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation_tt
		tooltip = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = high_velocity_irrigation_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { province_with_farm_goods = yes }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = high_velocity_irrigation_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = { remove_province_modifier = high_velocity_irrigation_mod }
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = high_velocity_irrigation_mod
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = high_velocity_irrigation_mod
	}
	penalties = {
		
	}
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.04
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

		artifice_has_points_30 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_mech_bureau_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_30 = yes
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { num_of_times_expanded_infrastructure = 1 }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_invention_mech_bureau_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_invention_mech_bureau_mod
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_invention_mech_bureau_mod
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_technomancy_influence = 0.06
		administrative_efficiency = 0.05
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_clockwork_rope_swingers
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_clockwork_rope_swingers
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = artifice_clockwork_rope_swingers
			duration = -1
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_clockwork_rope_swingers
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_clockwork_rope_swingers_tt
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			remove_country_modifier = artifice_clockwork_rope_swingers
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_clockwork_rope_swingers_tt
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		#update_artifice_points = yes #is included in the above effect
	}
	penalties = { }
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		siege_ability = 0.1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

#Mechanim
artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
		}
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_industrial_automatories }
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_allowed } }
			custom_tooltip = gain_access_to_automatory
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_allowed
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = mechanim_spread_country
				value = 0
			}
			set_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_working_privilege
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			clr_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_working_privilege
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
			clr_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_working_privilege
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.02
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 15
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_country_modifier = human_administration 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_memory_module
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
		}
		capital_scope = {
			continent = oceania
		}
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_memory_module.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = mechanim } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_memory_module_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = artifice_memory_module_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = artifice_memory_module_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.02
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 60
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				over_artifice_capacity = yes
				NOT = {
					any_owned_province = {
						has_building = automatory
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		artifice_granted_20 = yes
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		remove_country_modifier = artifice_mechanim_regiments_modifier
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		remove_country_modifier = artifice_mechanim_regiments_modifier
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.04
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 20
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			num_of_rajput = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				over_artifice_capacity = yes
				NOT = {
					num_of_rajput = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
artifice_invention_auto_scribes = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_auto_scribes
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
			capital_scope = {
				continent = oceania
			}
		}
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_30 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_auto_scribes.tt
		artifice_granted_30 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = mechanim }
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_auto_scribes_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = artifice_auto_scribes_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_30 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = artifice_auto_scribes_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.06
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				over_artifice_capacity = yes
				NOT = {
					any_owned_province = {
						has_building = automatory
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
#Gene Magic
artifice_invention_crop_enlarge = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
		}
		has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge.tt
		custom_tooltip = artifice_unforeseen_consequences.tt
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = fungi
					trade_goods = grain
					trade_goods = serpentbloom
					trade_goods = wine
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_crop_enlarge_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_crop_enlarge_modifier
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = artifice_crop_enlarge_modifier }
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_crop_enlarge_modifier
		}
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = artifice_crop_enlarge_modifier }
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_crop_enlarge_modifier
		}
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_brilliance_influence = 0.02
		supply_limit_modifier = 0.15
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 60
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 7
				OR = {
					trade_goods = fungi
					trade_goods = grain
					trade_goods = serpentbloom
					trade_goods = wine
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}
