artifice_invention_tgs_farmland = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_tgs_farmland
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
			capital_scope = {
				continent = oceania
			}
		}
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_tgs_farmland.tt
		custom_tooltip = artifice_unforeseen_consequences.tt
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				province_with_arable_goods = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_manufactory_no_custom_tooltip_trigger = yes }
				remove_province_modifier = artifice_tgs_farmland_modifier
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_tgs_farmland2_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = artifice_tgs_farmland_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_tgs_farmland2_modifier
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_tgs_farmland_modifier
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_tgs_farmland2_modifier
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_tgs_farmland_modifier
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_tgs_farmland2_modifier
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_tgs_farmland_modifier
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_brilliance_influence = 0.02
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 60
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 7
				province_with_arable_goods = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

		}

		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}

	on_invalid = {
		remove_country_modifier = mechanim_chassis_waterproof_modifier
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = artifice_has_chassis_selected
		}
	}

	penalties = { }

	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {

		}
	}
}

	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00

	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = artifice_invention_steel_tracking.tt
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.04
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				over_artifice_capacity = yes
				NOT = { num_of_colonists = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_mech_amphibious_attachements = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq2
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_mech_amphibious_attachements
		has_country_modifier = mechanim_military
	}

	can_select = {
		hidden_trigger = { ai = yes }
		artifice_has_points_10 = yes
	}

	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_10 = yes
	}

	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_10 = yes
	}

	penalties = { }
	
	benefits = {
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
		tec_mechanists_influence = 0.02
		allowed_marine_fraction = 0.25
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}
################
artifice_invention_rapid_fermentation = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq1
	max_absolutism = 0
	loyalty = 0.00
	influence = 0 #artificer privileges must never affect influence due to the fact influence affects points
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_rapid_fermentation
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_rapid_fermentation
		}
	}
	can_select = {
        ai = yes
		artifice_has_points_20 = yes
	}
	can_revoke = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_increase = yes
		}
		artifice_granted_20 = yes
		custom_tooltip = A80_rapid_fermentation_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_subject_other_than_tributary_trigger = yes }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = A80_rapid_fermentation
					duration = -1
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							trade_goods = wine
							trade_goods = grain
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = A80_rapid_fermentation_prov
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = wine
					trade_goods = grain
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = A80_rapid_fermentation_prov
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = { remove_province_modifier = A80_rapid_fermentation_prov }
	}
	on_revoked = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
		custom_tooltip = A80_rapid_fermentation_tt_revoke
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_rapid_fermentation } }
				remove_country_modifier = A80_rapid_fermentation
				every_owned_province = {
					remove_province_modifier = A80_rapid_fermentation_prov
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = A80_rapid_fermentation_prov
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			artifice_inventions_currently_used_decrease = yes
		}
		artifice_remove_20 = yes
		custom_tooltip = A80_rapid_fermentation_tt_revoke
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_rapid_fermentation } }
				remove_country_modifier = A80_rapid_fermentation
				every_owned_province = {
					remove_province_modifier = A80_rapid_fermentation_prov
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = A80_rapid_fermentation_prov
	}
	penalties = {}
	benefits = {
		global_unrest = -2
		ae_impact = -0.1
		artificers_privilege_slots = 1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}

artifice_invention_plant_grown_animals = {
	icon = Artf_Uniq1
	max_absolutism = 0

	on_revoked_province = {

	on_invalid = {

		hidden_effect = {

				every_owned_province = {

				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = A80_plant_grown_animals_prov

	penalties = {}
	benefits = {
		land_morale = 0.05
		land_attrition = -0.2

	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			over_artifice_capacity = yes
		}
	}
}
